Important News

8th Regular Meeting of the National Government

Resolved to Establish a Flood Relief Committee

Posthumous State Funeral for Former President Tan Set for September 4th

The 8th Regular Meeting of the National Government was held on the 14th, attended by committee members Yu Youren, Ye Chucang, Shao Yuanchong, Ma Fuxiang, Wang Boqun, Wang Zhengting, Ding Weifen, and Dai Chuanxian, with Yu Youren presiding. Matters discussed: (1) Dai Chuanxian, President of the Examination Yuan and Chief Examiner of the First Higher Examination, reported that after the completion of the examination and the issuance of certificates, it was discovered that one candidate, Liu Xizhang, in the examination for diplomatic and consular officials, had his average score for the first and second exams mistakenly calculated as 51 points instead of the correct 56 points. As a result, he was unable to receive the additional points required to pass. Upon discovery, Dai Chuanxian was deeply dismayed. Although the error was due to the extreme fatigue of the calculation staff, it was ultimately Dai Chuanxian's own fault for inadequate planning. He therefore urgently reported the facts, requesting the government to severely punish Dai Chuanxian for his poor management, in order to uphold the law and discipline. It was resolved that Liu Xizhang, as well as Tu Jin, who was unable to attend the third exam due to flood obstruction as stated in a separate report, should have their cases handled separately according to a prescribed procedure and submitted for review. Regarding Dai Chuanxian's request for self-punishment, Yu Youren, Ye Chucang, and Ding Weifen were assigned to conduct a preliminary review. (2) Committee Member Song Ziwen proposed: "The floods in various provinces this year are unprecedented in a century. The government bears a heavy responsibility. Despite the ongoing suppression of the Red Army and the shortfall in tax revenue, we dare not fail to exert our utmost efforts to cope with the situation. Yesterday, 2 million yuan in treasury bonds were allocated to the Disaster Relief Committee for emergency relief. However, the disaster is extraordinarily severe. To plan for the overall situation and seek widespread relief, it is proposed to establish a special disaster relief organization dedicated to this task, paying attention to the following points: 1. Investigation: Based on reliable reports and aerial reconnaissance, clarify the actual situation in each disaster area. 2. Fundraising: In addition to issuing public bonds, solicit donations from home and abroad, and purchase wheat to provide relief. 3. Rehabilitation: Provide farmers with seeds for spring planting next year and use this opportunity to repair dikes for disaster relief. From my observation, fundraising and wheat purchase seem to be easier to implement. However, how to conserve resources and effectively provide benefits to the victims is the most difficult question. It is best to adopt scientific methods of relief used in Europe and America to avoid wasting funds and ensure tangible results. We respectfully request your review and implementation." It was resolved that a Flood Relief Committee should be established, with Song Ziwen, Xu Shiying, Liu Shangqing, Kong Xiangxi, and Zhu Qinglan appointed as committee members, with Song Ziwen serving as chairman. (3) The Office of the Posthumous State Funeral for President Tan reported: "The Office convened the first joint meeting of the State Funeral Committee and the Engineering Committee on the 12th of this month and resolved the following matters: 1. Regarding the date of the state funeral, it is proposed to set it for September 4th of this year. 2. Regarding the state funeral protocol, in addition to the existing State Funeral Law and State Funeral Ritual, several supplementary protocols have been drafted with reference to the State Funeral Ritual for your review and record. 3. Regarding the state funeral expenses, it is proposed to instruct the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Finance to allocate the full amount in advance. 4. Regarding the state funeral eulogy, it is proposed to request your esteemed government to issue it in order to honor the occasion." It was resolved to follow the instructions and proceed accordingly. (4) It was resolved that Shui Zi, a counselor of the government, has been appointed to another position, and the vacancy will be filled by Hai Tao. (5) It was resolved to appoint Yan Dun as the Chief of Staff of the 7th Army Division.

Details of Yan's Return to Shanxi

Taking the route from Dalian via Shenyang and the Ping-Sui Railway

Disguised in a kimono and as a villager during the journey

Future itinerary undecided, appears calm

Taiyuan Correspondence: Yan Xishan's return to his native province via Dalian was reported in yesterday's news, but details were not given as officials had not formally announced it. Today, the Taiyuan Garrison Headquarters invited reporters to announce the details of Yan's return to Shanxi from Dalian. It was stated that he traveled by train, not by plane, which differs slightly from what people from Datong have said. Public attention has been focused on Yan's attitude. The reporter presents the findings of the investigation as follows:

The Journey Back to Shanxi: Yan Xishan, accompanied by Dr. Jin Ruixuan, departed Dalian by train at 9:30 PM on the 3rd of this month. At 7:00 AM on the 4th, the train arrived in Liaoning. After disembarking, he exchanged greetings with several old friends who were waiting for him and then went to the Tokiwa Hotel to rest. After a meal, he boarded the BeiNing train at 10:20 AM and arrived at Fengtai at 10:35 PM. He rested at the Tianhe Inn, west of the station, for over an hour and then took the PingSui train at 11:40 PM. At 3:50 AM on the 5th, he arrived in Datong and rested briefly at a certain mansion. He then took a long-distance bus to Huairen County, where he was met by a private car from the Hebian Village, which he then boarded. At 3:00 PM on the 6th, he arrived at Hebian Village and went to his private residence to rest.

After Arriving in Shanxi: After Yan arrived in Datong, the generals here heard about it. Zhou Dai, commander of the artillery, paid a visit by private car on the morning of the 6th. At noon the next day, Zhang Huizhao, deputy commander of the garrison, also paid a visit by car. Xu Yongchang, Yang Aiyuan, Sun Chu, and others also arrived by car one after another in the evening to have a long conversation with Yan. The content was mostly reminiscing about their separation. Generals Li Fuying, Feng Pengzhu, Yang Yaofang, and others also traveled by car yesterday to pay a visit. Feng, Yang, Li, Sun, and others returned to Taiyuan this afternoon.

Telegrams to Chiang and Zhang: Yan stated that his return to Shanxi was to visit his relatives. Yesterday, he officially telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Chiang and Deputy Commander Zhang, stating that he had safely arrived in his native Wutai County on the 6th of this month. It is known that Zhao Daiwen, Liang Ruzhou, Sun Huanlun, and others who accompanied Yan to Dalian are still living at No. 263, Section 4, Black Rock Reef in Dalian because the air there is excellent and it is a suitable place to escape the summer heat.

Yan's Attitude: Yan Xishan's sudden return has led to various speculations and conflicting opinions. Some say he is passive, while others say he is active. Those who care about the current situation are all eager to inquire. According to a certain person, Yan himself stated that he was returning to Shanxi to visit his relatives and that his attitude was clearly expressed and did not need to be elaborated upon. However, in my personal judgment, he would not sell out his friends for personal gain, or there may be other private matters.

Rumors of Yan's Visit to Taiyuan: It is rumored that Yan plans to take advantage of his return home to visit his friends in Taiyuan in the coming days to reminisce about their separation. Yan also told the friends who visited Hebian yesterday that he would visit them in Taiyuan. It is reported that a company from the guard battalion has been dispatched to Hebian for security.

Conversation with Escort: Yesterday, the reporter visited Dr. Jin Ruixuan, who accompanied Yan, to inquire about Yan's return to Shanxi. According to Jin, Yan received a telegram from home on the 2nd, stating that his father was ill and hoping that he would return to visit. Yan was very anxious after receiving the telegram and could not sleep well that night. The next morning, Yan suddenly asked Jin if he would take a risk with him and return home to visit his father and treat his illness. Jin immediately agreed and expressed his willingness to accompany him. Preparations were then made for the journey. That evening (the 3rd), Jin, carrying only a handbag, left the residence with Yan, claiming to be going to the beach. At 9:30 PM, they purchased two first-class train tickets and boarded the train, leaving Dalian. Yan was wearing Chinese clothing. At 6:30 AM on the 4th, they arrived in Liaoning and stayed at the Tokiwa Hotel. At 10:20 AM, Yan changed into a Japanese kimono and purchased two first-class tickets for the BeiNing train. There was already a Japanese person in the car. Jin, who had studied in Japan for many years and was proficient in Japanese, began speaking to the Japanese person in Japanese. As a result, the passengers in the car assumed that Yan and Jin were both Japanese, so no one paid attention to them. No one questioned them along the way. At 10:30 AM on the 5th, they arrived in Fengtai and rested at the Tianhe Inn for an hour. Yan disguised himself as a villager and purchased third-class tickets for the PingSui train. At 3:50 AM that night, they arrived in Datong and rested briefly at a certain mansion. They then took a long-distance bus back to Hebian. When they arrived in Huairen County, they were met by Yan's car and transferred to it. At 3:00 PM on the 6th, they arrived at Hebian. When Yan arrived home, his father was lying in bed, suffering from old age. Because of his advanced age and weakness, his appetite was poor, so his condition seemed slightly worse. I (Jin) took his pulse, prescribed medicine, and left that night from Yan's residence by car to the provincial capital. Jin plans to go to Hebian again tomorrow to visit Yan's father. Jin Ruixuan, courtesy name Xiangyuan, is a doctor of medicine from Huguan County in this province. He used to be a professor at Hebei University. He followed Yan to Dalian last year and returned to Shanxi with Yan this time.

Itinerary Undecided: According to those who returned from visiting Yan in Wutai, Yan said little about the current situation to the visitors, except to reminisce about their separation. When asked about his future itinerary, Yan only said that he would decide in a few days. Judging from his attitude, he seems very calm. Yan departed from Datong with Zhao Chengzhou and others at approximately 7:00 AM on the 6th. When they arrived at Yuanping Town in Guoxian County, Zhang Peimei, the former garrison commander of Southern Shanxi, and others were waiting at the station to greet him. Yan invited Zhang to ride in the car with him back to Hebian. Li Fuying and others from Xinxian also came to greet him by car. Yan was wearing a white linen summer shirt, a flat-topped wide-brimmed white straw hat, white socks, and black shoes, and he looked quite energetic (10th).

Shi Yousan Has Left Shandong

Han Fuju Has Sent Personnel to Verify Shi's Troops

Jinan Correspondence: Since the collapse of Shi Yousan's army, there have been various rumors about his whereabouts. According to reliable sources, Shi himself did indeed leave Shandong eastward on the night of the 10th. The route he took, whether by boat from Qingdao, Yantai, or Yangjiaogou, is still unknown. However, it is reported that he first went to Dalian and then to Japan. The scattered soldiers of Shi's army who fled to Shandong have all been concentrated in Linyi, awaiting verification and reorganization. The organization of a division has been confirmed, and Cheng Xixian will be appointed as the division commander. The announcement will be made as soon as Han Fuju requests the Central Government to issue a formal appointment. Cao Fulin, the commander-in-chief of the Third Army Corps, recently came to Jinan to report to Han on the number of Shi's scattered soldiers who fled to Shandong and their concentration in Linyi to await reorganization. Han expressed his satisfaction and ordered Cao to work with Cheng Xixian to be responsible for the reorganization. Cao returned from Jinan to Yucheng by Taishan armored train early on the 11th and then proceeded to Linyi. The personnel from the quartermaster and ordnance departments were prepared to distribute supplies according to the actual number of people verified and to prepare a roster to be submitted to the Central Government. If any firearms were missing, they would be replenished after verification. According to Ji Rongtao, the commander of the special service regiment of Shi's army who came to Shandong, he came to Jinan from Linyi last night (the 10th) with regiment commander Bi Wenshan to report to Chairman Han on their arrival in Linyi. The regiment commander paid a personal visit to the chairman early this morning (the 11th) and will return to Linyi within a few days. After the regiment arrived in Linyi, the regiment headquarters was set up outside the South Gate, and the soldiers were stationed outside the city. The city defense is still being handled by the original garrison, led by Commander Li (11th).

False Rumors of Entering Hunan

He Jian Prepares to Intercept at Hengbao

Changsha Correspondence: After receiving reports from the front lines that the Guangdong-Guangxi armies were invading Hunan in three routes, He Jian not only forwarded a request to Commander-in-Chief Chiang for the immediate dispatch of large forces to Hunan for assistance but also ordered Tao Guang's entire force to concentrate in Hengzhou to defend the key points. Yesterday, on the 8th, He Jian also received telegrams from Yongming and Lingling counties reporting the actions of Zhang Gui's army: (1) Tang Mengren, the magistrate of Yongming County, telegraphed that about 1,000 troops from Zhang Fakui's unit were attempting to attack the county seat. (2) Hu Tianxiang, the magistrate of Lingling County, reported that the advance detachment of Tan Lianfang's division of the Guangxi army, stationed at Shaziping, entered Hunan via Yangridu and Huangshahe, reaching Zhuozhu ao, 70 li from Yongzhou. Commander-in-Chief Chiang also telegraphed that the Guangdong-Guangxi invasion of Hunan was in response to Shi Yousan. Now that Shi had been completely resolved, any further invasion would be self-destructive. He had already prepared to dispatch five divisions to Hunan to provide assistance (August 9th).

Hubei Flood Disaster

Millions of Refugees

Various Counties Still Report Disasters

Losses Exceed Tens of Millions

Investigation of Responsibility Issues

Hankou Correspondence: The floods in Hubei Province have lasted for many days, with the province's economic heartland almost completely devastated. Reports of disasters from various counties continue to pour in. The severity of the disasters and the extent of the affected areas are truly unprecedented. The disaster situation in various counties is further detailed below.

In recent days, dozens of counties have reported disasters. The most severely affected include Yunmeng County, where over seventy embankments were flooded, with over fifty submerged. In Xiaogan County, all embankments and dikes have collapsed. In Qianjiang County, over one hundred out of one hundred and fifty embankments have been submerged. In Yingcheng County, all dikes and embankments have been breached, causing flooding for hundreds of miles. In Qishui County, the North Yonggan Dike and Yonggu Branch Dike have collapsed, and the Yongbao Dike has also been affected, leading to the submersion of the entire county. In Songzi County, two out of four districts have been completely submerged. In Shishou County, over ten thousand mu of farmland have been flooded. In Mianyang County, all river dikes have collapsed, and the entire city of Xindi has become a swamp. In Huanggang County, all embankments have collapsed. In Hanchuan County, many dikes and embankments have collapsed, and those that have not collapsed have been submerged by accumulated water. In Xianning County, lake water has overflowed, submerging all crops. In Anlu County, mountain floods have erupted, washing away fields and houses. In Luotian County, floods have spread, submerging farmland. In Yangxin County, river water has flowed backward, submerging the northeast, central, and southern townships. In Huangmei County, river dikes have collapsed, and all private embankments have been breached, affecting 200,000 people. In Zhongxiang County, the Huhe and Liangxiang townships have been submerged. In Jiangling County, the Cenhekou area has been flooded. In Tianmen County, the dikes below Yuekou have all collapsed, turning everything into ruins, and there is no way to travel through the east, west, and south townships. In Qichun County, the Yongbao and Yonggu dikes have collapsed, submerging an area of approximately eighty li, with all houses collapsed. In Guangji County, river water has flowed backward. In Luocheng County, eighteen embankments outside the dike and thirty-six embankments inside the dike have collapsed, submerging an area of hundreds of li. In Huangpi County, the eastern, western, and southern areas along the river, spanning over sixty li in all directions, have become a swamp. In Echeng County, over ninety zhang of river dike have collapsed, submerging over ten thousand mu of farmland, collapsing thousands of houses, and causing property losses of over three hundred thousand yuan. In Jiayu County, seven or eight places of official and private embankments have collapsed. The entire county of Gong'an has been submerged. The northwest along the river in Sui County has also been submerged, with water depths of over one zhang in flat areas. In Jianli County, the Xindi dike has breached, and river water has flowed backward into the entire county. The entire county of Yun County has been submerged. In Dangyang County, mountain water has erupted, and the entire county has suffered from the disaster. In Zhijiang County, the areas along the river have been flooded, suffering severe damage. The above information is based on investigations by the Department of Civil Affairs. The disaster situation is relatively mild and those that have not been reported are not included. Approximately tens of thousands of mu of farmland have been submerged, affecting millions of people, and the losses exceed tens of millions of yuan.

The Hubei Provincial Government and the Flood Relief Committee have repeatedly appealed to Chairman Chiang, the Executive Yuan, the Central Relief Committee, and the authorities of various provinces since the occurrence of the flood, sending numerous urgent letters and telegrams. They also negotiated with the Pinghan Railway Bureau, the Special Tax Bureau, and the Unified Tax Bureau to collect additional surcharges on their behalf and issued orders to all agency staff to reduce their salaries uniformly to continue providing relief. Furthermore, due to the large number of victims and the vast disaster area, it was decided to send personnel to various counties to conduct on-site investigations and comfort the affected people. The City Party Department Rectification Committee also convened temporary meetings with representatives from various district party departments, trade associations, and labor unions to discuss relief measures, resulting in the decision on several important cases: (1) request the municipal government to send people to investigate flooded areas daily, prevent house collapses, and order district party departments and mass organizations to report any issues in a timely manner; (2) request the provincial and municipal governments to promptly block the collapsed dikes; (3) request the relief committee and the Public Security Bureau to ban rescue ships from demanding ferry fares; (4) request the municipal government to build wooden bridges to help pedestrians; (5) request the relief committee to strictly prohibit relief personnel from committing violence against disaster victims and ensure widespread distribution of aid; (6) request the garrison department to prevent hooligans from dismantling flooded houses; (7) request the disaster prevention office and the relief committee to provide relief to refugees in the Zongguan area and protect dams. In addition, increasing refugee shelters, ordering refugees to move, and transporting refugees back to their hometowns are all underway separately.

Regarding the issue of responsibility for this flood, all parties are paying close attention, and various newspapers have also discussed it from time to time. He Chengjun, the chairman of the province, also intended to thoroughly investigate. The disaster was extremely severe, and the responsible personnel failed to prevent it in advance and failed to respond effectively in an emergency, wasting national funds and harming the people. If they are not severely punished, it will not be enough to appease public anger and warn those in the future. However, He Chengjun stated in his report at the provincial government's memorial week on the tenth that the issue of responsibility cannot be blamed on others, roughly saying, "The recent flood is unprecedented in sixty years. Whether it is due to inadequate human prevention is still under investigation. However, according to numerous reports and my own on-site investigation, it cannot be blamed on others. However, since the news media raised the issue of responsibility, some wanted to use this to attack or deceive, and others with political ambitions took this opportunity to push others off the stage so that they could obtain a considerable position. I have long known about this situation. Today, I originally intended to issue a warning, but friends repeatedly advised me that for every foot the Dao rises, the Devil rises ten feet. Therefore, I can only move forward with enthusiasm and determination, defeat all demons, clarify right and wrong, distinguish truth from falsehood, and rectify people's hearts, so as not to harm society and the country." (August 11)

Rapid Increase in Yangtze River Water Volume

The Three Towns are in Rescue Efforts for Days

Hankou Merchants and People Lost Four Million

Hankou Correspondence: The Yangtze River's water level had slightly stabilized since the tenth, and on the eleventh morning, it even receded by an inch or so. The people of Wuhan were celebrating their recovery when, on the evening of the same day, the north wind roared, heavy rain poured down, trees were uprooted, houses collapsed, and the river water continued to rise. On the twelfth and thirteenth, it continued to rise without stopping, reaching a maximum depth of fifty-one feet, five inches, and five points, making the situation even more serious. According to a certain engineer familiar with the water situation, if it rises another eight inches, the three towns of Wuhan will be submerged. The future disaster is even more alarming. I don't know what the authorities will do to deal with the aftermath. The current rescue situation in the three towns is recorded as follows:

Hankou: The dikes and dams in various places have been greatly affected by the water in recent days, all showing dangerous signs, especially the dikes from Qiaokou to Zongguan in Hankou, which are the most dangerous. There are three dikes here, all ending at Qiaokou. The first is the Sichuan-Hankou Railway subgrade, the second is the Zhanggong Dike, and the third is the Huangjingtang Dike. The Sichuan-Hankou Railway subgrade and the Zhanggong Dike are to prevent the water from the Houhu Lake, the height of the dikes are equal, and the distance is also close. The Huangjingtang Dike is an extension of the Pinghan Railway line, and the distance is also close. The Huangjingtang Dike is an extension of the Pinghan Railway line, specifically to prevent the Xiang River. It is about four feet lower than the Zhanggong Dike. After the renovation, it is only a few inches higher than the river water. Because the Xiang River is calm, it has not collapsed. The Sichuan-Hankou Railway subgrade is close to the flood, and there is accumulated water inside. When the wind was raging on the twelfth, the section of the road from the Pacific Soap Factory to the section of 1312, which is about two li long, was flooded, which was very dangerous. After the municipal government engineering team made every effort to block it, they nailed wooden stakes on the slope of the roadbed, and then added burlap sacks. After a few hours, the waves calmed down a bit and the work was completed, and the danger was turned into safety. The Zhanggong Dike was also protected.

Wuchang: The most dangerous is the Chopsticks Street under Hanyangmen, followed by the Jiangdi River at Datikou, Xujiapeng and other places, and the Lakedi Dam of Saihu Lake. On the thirteenth, a mouth suddenly broke in the Chopsticks Street section, and the river water poured in. The Construction Department sent workers to rescue, and the breach was blocked. The Datikou, Xujiapeng, and Lakedi dams also built sandbags according to the height of the water, and no accidents occurred. However, the sub-dike of the Wuqing Dam, Binsan Dam, was submerged by water, so the nearby Babu Street, Xinqiao, and Xiang'e Road tracks were flooded, but the dam has not been broken. If it is quickly heightened and thickened, it can still block the water.

Hanyang: The embankments in the Heishan, Yangjiahe, and Nan'anzui areas are also in danger. The Disaster Prevention Office has ordered the county government to quickly rescue them, and ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau to send personnel to assist. If the water does not rise again, there may be no worries.

The drainage project in Hankou City started to build wooden dikes on the seventh, and the starting line was completed on the tenth. It was originally scheduled to drain the accumulated water in the city by the twelfth or at the latest fourteenth. Because the north wind suddenly rose and the waves surged like mountains, the wooden dikes along the river were broken by the water, and the original trees were uprooted. The unbroken wooden dikes were submerged by rising water and lost their effectiveness. The drainage plan had to be abandoned. However, the Disaster Prevention Office is still continuing. Yesterday, the Hanxingchang Construction Factory, which contracted the project, was ordered to quickly repair the damaged dams and unfinished projects, and start pumping water on a specified date, and sent personnel to the Electricity Bureau of the Third Special Zone (the former British Concession) to borrow water windmills for use. It is said that each of these windmills can pump 300,000 gallons of water per hour. If the dams are built and the river water does not rise, the drainage plan still has hope of being completed. Moreover, the commercial affairs in Hankou were greatly affected by the flood. The losses of merchants and people are countless. In terms of compensation expenses alone, the daily loss is about 300,000 yuan. The disaster has lasted for more than ten days, and the total loss is 4 million yuan. Including various losses, I am afraid it will not be less than tens of millions of yuan. It can also be seen that the suffering is deep. (August 13)

Gannannan Red Bandits Were Cut in Two

Communication Between Xingtai and Xingyu Districts Lost

Three Route Army Advances on Yudu, Fierce Fighting With Bandits

Nanchang Correspondence: After the Suppression Army recovered Donggu, the Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang factions retreated to Xingguo, Yudu, Ruijin, and Huichang, echoed the bandits on the Fujian border, and planned to enter western Jiangxi via Xingguo and Taihe to avoid the Suppression Army's offensive. However, the Suppression Army suddenly recovered Xingguo, and the bandits were cut in two. According to the reconnaissance report by the plane, the main force of the bandits is in the Guanxi and Shacun areas west of Xingguo and east of Taihe, with about tens of thousands of people. They are currently being monitored by the divisions of Gong Bingfan, Luo Lin, and Cai Tingkai. They can't advance and can't retreat. One is in the areas of Liantang north of Yudu and Liangcun and Guantian north of Yongfeng and south of Xingguo, with no less than tens of thousands of people. They are the fake Thirty-Fifth Army of Deng Yigang, the fake Third Army of Huang Gonglue, and the fake Fourth Army of Lin Biao, but they come out at night and dare not engage the Suppression Army. Currently, the Sun Lianzhong Division of the Suppression Army is in Gulonggang, the Shangguan Yunxiang Division is in Longgang, and the Zhao Guantao Division is in Xingguo, all besieging the bandits. They encountered tens of thousands of bandits near Liantang and Liangcun between Yu and Xing. From dawn to dusk, they fought fiercely for several days, charging back and forth, and the two sides fought in close combat. The intensity of the battle was unprecedented. Later, because the bandits lacked bullets, they mostly used spears and swords to charge. The Suppression Army also fought back with box cannons and broadswords, and finally defeated the bandits. It is said that the Third Route Army rested for a while and continued to advance triumphantly to Yudu. (August 11)

He has come to China from Tokyo and arrived in Shenyang at 6:40 am on the tenth to take up his new post. More than 20 other new employees also came to take up their posts. After Kimura arrived in Shenyang, he will visit Chinese and foreign agencies with the new staff to express his opinions. His speech is as follows: "Mantetsu has established the Fengtian Office this time for two major reasons. One is internal, that is, the original Mantetsu Office, Local Office, Transportation Office, and other offices in Fengtian, and various agencies will be added in the future. If there is no unified agency, it will be very inconvenient to contact each other. One is external, that is, Fengtian is an important city, and all agencies must be unified. There is a foreign agency representing Mantetsu. The Fengtian Office is based on the above two major reasons to decide to re-establish it. However, the necessity of the office depends on how people handle it. I (Kimura called himself) am determined to do my best to handle it well and exert its functions. I plan to stay here for the time being, and in the future, I will spend four days a week in Fengtian and three days in Dalian, so that the Fengtian Office can be closely connected with the head office. From now on, in addition to supervising the local office and the railway office, it will also take charge of foreign negotiations, and the railway negotiations are the same. When the time comes, it should start." (August 10)

People from Huaiyang

Establish a Water Conservancy Committee

Solve the Current Predicament Together Regardless of Borders

Yangzhou Correspondence: The upper and lower reaches of the canal and the banks along the river are flooded with water in more than 20 counties at the same time. Millions of lives will be in danger. People from all over Yang are very anxious. Therefore, Dai Tianqiu, Yang Jiaru, etc. invited people with more canal-based labor insurance experience from Huaiyang at 2 pm yesterday (13th) to discuss emergency methods and advise the authorities so that there would be no damage to the upper and lower reaches. The meeting address is temporarily borrowed from Dai Tianqiu's private residence. A total of 23 people attended, including Xu Shuhou, Chen Shiyi (Huaiyin), Hao Xingheng, Hao Weihou (Huaian), Liu Lingsheng, Lu Shao Liu (Baoying), Qiao Boyao (Yancheng), Guo Yinhuai, Li Jichen (Xinghua), Yuan Luzhong, Yuan Chengde (Dongtai), Ruan Lianzhong, Bao Xiangzhong (Yizheng), Wang Jingting, Dai Tianqiu, Yang Jiaru, Hu Xianbo, Zhang Shushen, Zhu Ganchen, Zhang Shaozhai, Zhou Xiangting, Chen Jingren, Zhang Dihua (Jiangdu), etc., researched for a long time, and unanimously advocated that the upper and lower reaches should not be considered as a watershed, and the overall goal is to save people's lives. The main points of the discussion were: (1) to suggest the disaster relief methods in the past to the provincial government and request them to adopt them; (2) to announce the road for draining into the sea, and stipulate that each county should elect two people to organize a water conservancy committee in Yangzhou, so that each county can exchange opinions at any time, and the organization method will be determined after submitting the plan to the party department for record. A document was drafted on the spot, requesting Chairman Ye and Director Zhang to order the coastal salt reclamation companies to open more dike gates and destroy each gate to facilitate the draining of water. As you indicated, the relationship between Zhaoba has been telegraphed to Commander Liang." (3) Commander Liang replied to people in the downstream telegram, "I have read your telegram. The issue of opening the Zhaoguan Dam belongs to local administration and should be the responsibility of local officials. This headquarters is only willing to do its best to protect the embankment and prevent disasters for the people." He is scheduled to continue to Guangfu Shenghua Yuetang and other townships today to survey the wilderness.

Suzhou

The Wanted Criminal in the Tong'an Bridge Robbery Case Was Arrested: Xu Yuheng, the son of famous doctor Xu Hedan, went to Jingshu this spring to sweep the tombs, and his relative Liu Yinxuan (a prominent local family) was robbed by bandits while visiting the Taihu Lake. Later, the Liu family received a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 30,000 yuan. They then transferred 11,000 yuan to Shen Shoutian, who was introduced by someone, to negotiate with the bandit den. As a result, Shen not only took the money, but also said that the bandit leader Qin Lao San demanded 200,000 yuan before he would release Liu and the others. Therefore, the family entrusted another person to take 14,500 yuan to redeem them. Xu and others were trapped in the bandits for 80 days. Recently, Zhu Mian, the commander of the Taihu Bandit Suppression, learned that Shen Shoutian was actually a disciple of Li Dayou, the leader of the Chaohu gang, who specialized in acting as a bandit line and negotiating ransom tickets for profit. Therefore, yesterday (14th), he devised a way to buy a line and arrested Shen. He confessed that he had defrauded 11,000 yuan and that he had also handled the case of the Tong'an Bridge robbery last year, in which the bandit washed and killed the business group coach Zhu Zuozhou and robbed ten people including teachers and businessmen. He was redeemed by businessmen Jin Peizhi and others for 5,000 yuan. He embezzled 2,000 yuan and so on. After the interrogation, he was immediately detained for instructions.

The Chamber of Commerce Sent a Letter Requesting Repairs to the Streets in the City: The County Chamber of Commerce, in view of the fact that the streets in the county have been in disrepair for many years, and the area is full of swamps after a rain. The construction funds of Wuxian County have accumulated a lot. Since it has been collected from the public, it should be used for the public. The city's streets have not been repaired since the street was widened from the 16th year of the Republic of China. Therefore, yesterday (14th), it sent a letter to the Construction Bureau, requesting that the accumulated funds be used to repair the streets in sections.

The Important Criminal in the Xu Zhuang Robbery Case Has Been Arrested: The Xu Zhuanjia, a farmer in the Hengqing Township, Zhuangluo Township, was robbed by bandits the night before, and three people were shot and injured. As mentioned in yesterday's newspaper, it is now known that Zhang Shousheng, a bandit living in the case, has been arrested by the Hengqing Public Security Bureau yesterday (14th). According to the confession, there are five or six accomplices who will take the train to Shanghai at Guandu Lane this evening. He immediately telegraphed the Public Security Bureau, ordering the First Branch to send members with the Criminal Investigation Team to Guandu Lane Station to investigate the remaining bandits.

Songjiang

The Chamber of Commerce Organizes a Free Clinic: At the last regular meeting of the county's Chamber of Commerce, it was suggested by Guo Leye that the Chamber should set up a free clinic every summer to help poor and sick people who cannot afford medical treatment. The proposal was approved and the clinic was organized accordingly. Local doctors of various specialties were hired, and on the first day of consultation (the 11th), the clinic was crowded with patients. In the future, consultations will be held on the 1st and 6th of each month to benefit the poor and sick.

Dismantling an Airplane Causes Further Complications: The white airplane under the jurisdiction of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force landed in Xinqiao the other day. This newspaper has reported on it repeatedly. It is now learned that the Shanghai Aircraft Factory sent personnel and 20 workers to Xinqiao yesterday to dismantle the aircraft and transport the parts back. Unexpectedly, the town refused to cooperate with the aircraft staff, agreeing not to provide food or lodging and prohibiting the dismantling of the aircraft. They then requested police protection. Unexpectedly, Han Xiaozhou, an assistant at the district office, came out to oppose it, almost leading to a conflict. Upon hearing the news, the county government's public security bureau immediately dispatched a police team and officers to Xinqiao to suppress the situation and took Han Xiaozhou to Songjiang. They went to the county government. It is said that County Magistrate Shen reprimanded the assistant in person.

Nantong

The Court Thoroughly Investigates the Water Police's Unauthorized Killing: Xie Zezhi, the captain of the provincial water police team stationed in Nantong, was stabbed by his former subordinate Yan Zheming. Yan fled to the front of the court, where he was caught up and shot dead by the water police team. The case is complicated. Yan Zheming's elder brother, Qingshan, came to Nantong to appeal to various parties. The court's prosecutor's office scheduled a preliminary hearing on the 9th to thoroughly investigate the case, summoning Xie Zezhi and officers Wang Fusheng, He Guochang, Xu Zhaobin, Zhang Baoshan, Wu Ruishun, and Lian Hanqing for interrogation. Yan Zheming is currently buried in the public cemetery in the east of the city, and his coffin will be opened for examination.

The Ministry of Transportation Sends a Commissioner to Survey the Riverbank: Due to the severe collapse of the Nantong riverbank, which greatly affects water conservancy and transportation, the Ministry of Transportation has appointed Li Eryi of the Yangtze River Waterway Regulation Commission to come to Nantong to conduct on-site surveys of the riverbank and water flow.

Business Tax Allocation Issues: Nantong's business tax is paid by the Chamber of Commerce at 8,000 yuan per quarter. There are still issues with the allocation of the tax among various industries. The Chamber of Commerce has appointed Li Yinong and six others to work with the business tax bureau to first investigate the capital amount and business volume of each store, and then discuss the allocation method.

Wuxi

The Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs a Request for Investigation of the Vandalism of the Cinema: The Wuxi Grand Theater in the city park was vandalized by twenty to thirty people wearing water police uniforms on the evening of the 12th, causing significant damage. Ticket collectors Xue Guangtao and Yu A’gen were also injured. The incident has been reported to the county court for examination of the injuries and investigation of the perpetrators. Yesterday, the court sent a letter to the county Chamber of Commerce stating that the rioters wore uniforms and armed belts, and after the riot, they gathered in the park for roll call, clearly intending to sabotage the business. The court requested the Chamber of Commerce to uphold justice and find a way to provide relief. The Chamber of Commerce approved the request, stating that the park is a public place, yet people dared to gather and commit violence. What about law and order? Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce telegraphed Shen Gaozhen, the district chief of the Second Water Police District, requesting him to personally come to Wuxi to investigate the case immediately, ensure the arrest of the perpetrators, and severely punish them, and not to simply listen to his subordinates and conduct a superficial investigation.

Two Robberies in Rural Areas in One Day: The crime of robbery is not decreasing in rural areas. The other day, two robberies occurred in one day. The details are recorded as follows: (1) In the area near Luo She, Wang Qiao, in the 16th district (Wananshi), Jiangbei resident Ping A’de lived in a thatched house and had some savings. The other night, four thugs suddenly came from the Yangshuyuan area, one with a pistol and three with flashlights. They broke down Ping's front door, tied up eleven men, women, and children with ropes, searched the house for an hour, and forcibly removed the gold earrings worn by Ping's wife and daughter, firing several shots before leaving. After the thugs entered, Ping had already escaped through the back door and ran to Yanjiadang Business Group to ask for help, but the robbers had already gone far. (2) In the Sheng'an area of Kaiyuan Township, Yuan Yingui and his five sons were all diligent and thrifty farmers, so they had some savings. Unexpectedly, around one o'clock yesterday morning, four robbers, two with flashlights and two with rifles, broke down the door and entered, driving Yuan and his sons into a corner of the room. One robber stood guard with a gun, while the other robbers searched everywhere. They robbed more than twenty yuan in cash, three fur robes, gold and silver jewelry, cotton-padded clothes, etc., with losses estimated at more than three hundred yuan.

Discovery of Triad Gangsters in Xin’an Town: Xin'an Town, in the 13th district (Xin'an Township), is lined with shops and densely populated. It has always been peaceful. Around seven o'clock the other night, more than forty triad gangsters suddenly arrived, traveling on four bandit boats from the direction of South Taihu Lake. They each carried weapons such as pistols, Mauser pistols, and iron rulers. After the bandit boats arrived in town, they swarmed ashore and posted sentries on the streets and alleys. At that time, the merchants and residents of the town were all cooling off on the streets when they suddenly saw the gangsters arrive. They sounded gongs to gather the crowd and prepared to resist the bandits. The water police patrol boat stationed in the town also prepared after hearing the alarm, but fearing that they would be outnumbered, they sent a messenger to report to the police brigade headquarters stationed in Wangting, and the third platoon of the first company sent police to assist. Seeing that the villagers were prepared, the bandit leader blew a whistle as a signal, assembled the team, robbed an empty boat from villager Pu A’da, and sped away. After receiving the report and arriving in town, the third platoon conducted a thorough search in the town, arrested a suspect named Wang Shouqing, and found a pistol and twelve bullets left behind by the gangsters in a nearby grave. They immediately took them back to the city yesterday and sent them to the first company to be interrogated by the brigade headquarters.

Successive Raids on Opium Dens: It is well known that there are many opium dens and opium smokers in the county. Although the county authorities have strictly prohibited them, the largest opium dens and well-known smokers are rarely caught. As a result, the area is filled with opium smoke. Ma A’quan, a resident of No. 32 Luhua Alley outside the North Gate, is a large opium den in the northern part of the city. During the tenure of former County Magistrate Sun Zuji, he was ordered by the province to arrest Ma A’quan and his wife and impose penalties. Unexpectedly, after Ma A’quan served his term, he reorganized and resumed his old business. The other night, Peng Xiwang, the chief of the fifth branch of the public security bureau in charge, learned of this and sent police to search Ma's house, seizing a jar of opium paste and a bag of opium ash from Ma Zifu's body. Ma A’quan and Ma Fubao were taken to the bureau, briefly interrogated, and then sent to the county public security bureau on the 14th, and then transferred to the county court for interrogation. In addition, County Magistrate Chen Chuande recently received a letter from Zou Sen reporting that there are two well-known opium dens on Guanqian Street in the city, which are very prosperous. He requested that police be dispatched to search them as soon as possible. County Magistrate Chen ordered Police Chief Wu Zhengrong to lead the police to search them. First, in Tang Zhu’s den (Tang Lao San) in the small teahouse at No. 5 Guanqian Street, they arrested ten opium offenders including Tang Zhuangkui (Tang Zhuping), and seized a large number of exhibits. Then, they raided an opium den east of the library and arrested fifteen opium offenders including Hua Yin and Fang A’shou. They were all sent to the county and, after interrogation by Wang Kaiwei, chief of the second section, a document was prepared to transfer them to the county court. Yesterday morning, after a preliminary hearing by Chief Justice Zhou, he ordered them all to be detained to await sentencing according to law.

Water Patrol Team Captures Thieves: Qian Tianxiong, the captain of the county water patrol team, recently brought plainclothes police officers to patrol the countryside due to the increasing number of robberies in the surrounding villages. At dawn the other day, near Dongting, they saw four people, each carrying a bundle, acting suspiciously. They immediately pursued and captured three of them. After interrogation, they confessed that one was Wang Heshang, from Wujin, one was Du Ronghe, and one was Lu Baolin, both from Jiangyin. They all confessed to breaking into the Hua family's house in Dongting and stealing because they had no money. They then confessed that there were still stolen goods in the mulberry field. Police officers were dispatched to search the address and found many items of clothing and mosquito nets. They have been sent to the brigade headquarters and then transferred to the county court for interrogation.

Progress on the Construction of the Ring Road around Taihu Lake: The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces previously planned to build a ring road around Taihu Lake through various counties. The Jiangsu Construction Department had already sent personnel to complete the survey, and the lakeside counties had made concrete plans. However, progress had been delayed due to the lack of confirmed funding. Recently, the Construction Department decided to actively raise funds to complete the project as soon as possible, and ordered Ye Jiajun, director of the provincial highway bureau, and the engineering department to take charge of the matter. Director Ye, upon receiving the order, deemed it necessary to investigate previous files in order to prepare the project budget. Yesterday, he sent letters to the construction bureaus of Wuxi, Wujin, and Yixing counties, requesting them to send the previous files on the ring road around Taihu Lake to the bureau to facilitate overall planning and promote progress.

Changzhou

District Chief Xie Leads Team to Capture Thieves: The house of Zhang Maobao, a resident of Dongji Township, the third district of Wuyi County, was robbed previously. One thief, Zhou Lianzi, had been captured. Another thief, Pan Lao San, was carrying the stolen goods the other day because the local crackdown was very strict. He took a boat from Xiaohe Town to Benniu, intending to take a bus to Shanghai to take temporary shelter. Xie Jun, the district chief of Xixiasu, the third district, was informed and immediately led the security team to wait at the ferry terminal. When the boat arrived, they went forward to search and captured Pan Lao San and many stolen goods. After a preliminary hearing in the district, he confessed to robbing Zhang Maobao's house. District Chief Xie sent the suspect to the city on the 13th to be interrogated by the Clean-Up Bureau.

Poisons Sent to the Procuratorate for Examination: A large amount of poisons such as morphine essence was found at Benniu Station in Wuyi County. Party and government agencies have requested the delivery of the goods and the detention of the people. On the morning of the 13th, Yang Kongxi, the chief prosecutor of the county court, and Li Zonggang, the chief of the public security bureau, went to Benniu by car. At that time, there were many disputes over the circumstances of the discovery of the poisons. Pan Yushu, the station chief, requested instructions from the Shanghai Police General Division. The prosecutor then took the goods to the procuratorate for investigation. County Magistrate Zhang Pengzhu also sent a telegram to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval.

Danyang

A Murder Case in Zangxiang Village: Tan Wangshi's son Jiaxing from Zangxiang Village in the western countryside was betrothed to Zhou Zhangshi's daughter Maomao from Zhouxiang Village since childhood. Because Jiaxing was young and studying outside, they were not yet married. His mother, Wangshi, suddenly contracted a serious illness and passed away this year, so he married Zhou and brought her into the family to take charge of household affairs. She was diligent and thrifty and was praised by her neighbors. Unexpectedly, Zhou committed suicide by hanging herself yesterday. After receiving the report, the county government sent a special investigator to investigate. According to her husband, Tan Jiaxing, Zhou led the cow back to her mother's house in Zhouxiang the day before to grind rice. She was careless on the way and the cow fell into the dung pit, causing her to be reprimanded by her mother, and she hanged herself out of shame and anger. Her mother accused the clan chief Tan Changming and others of bullying her and causing her daughter to commit suicide out of shame and anger. County Magistrate Wang believed that the case was serious and is under investigation.

Zhenjiang

Huai'an and Baoying Embankments Report Emergencies Simultaneously: County Magistrate Lin Jing of Huai'an telegraphed the province yesterday, stating that the dikes of the Huai'an Canal have been immersed in water for a long time. Although sub-dikes have been built, there are still many leaks, especially in four places: Banzha Town, Beijiaolou, Nanjiaozhen, and Sanyudong. They have been rushing to plug the leaks day and night, and have repaired the plum blossom area in Banzha Town Beijiao. The rest are still being plugged. In addition, the Jiangsu Water Conservancy Bureau received a telegram yesterday from Chief Engineer Pei, stationed at the post office, stating that the Huailouwan embankment in Baoying had collapsed for more than a li. Director Li has supervised workers to rush to plug the leak, and has requested the purchase of 3,000 hemp bags, which have been rushed to be shipped by the Yichun steamship for emergency use. As of the 13th, the water level at Yumatai was still reported to be stable at 1 zhang 9 chi 2 cun. The water level in Bengbu fell another 2 centimeters on the 12th, with a water level of 19 meters 52.

Jiaxing

Various Businesses Request the Dismissal of the Stamp Duty Bureau Chief: Chen Jun, the chief of the Jiaxing Stamp Duty Bureau, is young and lazy and does not often go to the bureau. The bureau affairs are handled by a certain clerk in the bureau, and the investigators are also recklessly harassing the people. Occasionally, when they discover underpaid or unpaid stamp duty, they impose severe fines. Merchants and residents are full of complaints. The various businesses have now jointly requested the county Chamber of Commerce to forward a request to the provincial bureau to immediately dismiss the bureau chief from his duties in order to maintain official integrity.

Please Remove the Fishing Company's Dam: The Xinji and Yutai fishing companies in the Shuangqiao area of Jiaxing have built dams in the nearby waterways, which are extremely strong. Not only do they hinder water conservancy, but they are also greatly related to farmland. During the recent flood, the farmers in the area requested that the dams be removed to release the water flow. The county government ordered Gao Derun, the chief of the county public security bureau, to supervise the removal of the upper dams of the two fishing companies. Unexpectedly, the farmers in the area again requested the county government to order the complete removal. County Magistrate Gong and Construction Bureau Chief Liang personally went to the countryside to conduct on-site inspections and confirmed that they did indeed hinder water conservancy. The dam built by Xinji was particularly strong and needed to be completely removed. Therefore, they requested the Construction Department to approve the request, and will order the complete removal after approval.

Please Prohibit the Leakage of Rice and Stone to the Sea: In Jiaxing, the price of rice has risen by more than two yuan in the last ten days, and there is a trend of continued increases. The Rice Industry Association and the Rice Price Review Council have requested the county government to forward a request to the provincial department to investigate and prohibit the leakage of rice from Pinghu, Xiashi, and Haining to the sea. After receiving the request, the county government has telegraphed the provincial government to request the appointment of a commissioner to be stationed in Pinghu, Xiashi, Haining, etc. to strictly investigate leakage to the sea in order to maintain the people's food supply.

Huzhou

Zheng Bingyi, a notorious bandit, is executed: Wang Zhiqi, commander of the Second Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team, received a secret order from the provincial government on the 9th, stating that Zheng Bingyi (aka Zheng Handa), the commander of the fourth company of the regiment, was colluding with bandits and sharing the spoils. He was ordered to be publicly executed immediately. At 8 a.m., he was executed by shooting within the regiment's headquarters. The vacancy was temporarily filled by Guo Jingzhi, the platoon leader of Zheng's former subordinates. Zheng was originally a notorious bandit. When Hang Yi was the commander two years ago, he repented and surrendered and was appointed as the commander of the guerrilla team. He was later appointed as the commander of the fourth company. The massive robbery case in Shimenwan last year and the robberies of ships that repeatedly occurred at Yangjiazhuang Dongqiaotou outside the West Gate were all committed by Zheng's former subordinates, which was confirmed to be related to Zheng. After investigation by the province, he was immediately executed. Afterwards, the entire city was under martial law, and shops closed early in the evening. The situation was unusually solemn.

Hangzhou

Xu Case: Ye Caizhen and Chen Yanxiang Released on Bail: In the case of the assassination of Xu Zhuoran in Fujian, after being transferred to the Hangzhou County Local Court for investigation and sentencing, Ye Caizhen, Chen Yanxiang, and Chen Delin were found to have insufficient evidence for the assassination and were all declared innocent. Only Lin Luo was sentenced to four years in prison for the crime of privately possessing military weapons. Subsequently, the original prosecutor appealed. The court opened on the 11th for review. The defendants Ye Caizhen and the other two requested bail. It is now learned that the judge Xie Hong’en, who was handling the case, stated that the case had been re-arrested with two suspects, Chen Chang and Zhang Jichang, who were highly suspected, and that Chen had confessed that he was present at the time of Xu's assassination. The suspicion of Ye Caizhen and others had been reduced, and it was specially ruled yesterday that each of them would be temporarily released on bail with a surety of 20,000 yuan from a substantial shop. Subsequently, the Overseas Chinese Chen Jiageng Company of Yangbatou, Hangzhou, guaranteed the release of Ye Caizhen and Chen Yanxiang, and was responsible for ensuring that they would be available whenever summoned, and guaranteed a bail of 40,000 yuan, which could be paid if ordered. As for Chen Delin, he is still looking for a guarantor and will be released on bail as soon as one is found. Ye and Chen were both discharged from the hospital in the afternoon.

A Major Bribery Case Cracked in Hangzhou: Zhang Jiaxian's mother, a resident of Changgang Town in the eastern countryside of Xiaoshan, was kidnapped by bandits last year and a letter was sent demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan. Later, the family tried their best to raise 19,500 yuan and entrusted Shen Baosheng, a fellow villager, to go to Shanghai to negotiate. Shen took advantage of this opportunity to profit from it, resulting in insufficient funds, and the victim was torn up by the bandits and her body was dumped in the river. Upon hearing the news, Zhang was extremely grief-stricken and reported to the County Clean-Up Bureau. One of the kidnappers, Qian Asong, was arrested, who confessed that Feng Binggang, a former detective team member, had received a bribe of 300 yuan, and Shen Baosheng had received 200 yuan, and they had now fled to the province. The provincial Clean-Up Bureau ordered the strict arrest. Shen Baosheng was arrested by the Provincial Public Security Bureau the other day. After a brief interrogation, he was transferred to the Army Prison for detention. Feng Binggang was also hiding in Hangzhou. Yesterday afternoon, he was detected by a secret agent from the fourth section of the Security Office, who tracked him to the entrance of Hu Zhengyuan Foreign Goods Store on Yanling Road and arrested him for investigation.

Impact of the Gunfire on the Gongsan Bus: Since the Gongsan section of the Hangzhou-Shaoxing Highway bus was shot the other day at dusk, passengers have felt quite dangerous. It is now learned that the Highway Administration believes that since the weather has become shorter since autumn, the last bus from Sanlangmiao to Hubin should be advanced by half an hour. It is scheduled to start today (the 15th) at 7:00 pm. Yesterday, all stations were notified to comply.

Ningbo

Yao County Elects Representatives to the Provincial Conference: The Fourth Zhejiang Provincial Congress of Representatives is about to open. The by-election of representatives from Yuyao was held at 3 p.m. yesterday. As a result, Ni Yongqiang and Yang Tianshou were elected as representatives. As for the preliminary election of representatives to the National Congress of Representatives, Ni Yongqiang was elected.

A Large Band of Local Bandits Discovered in Wangjiashan: The Fengxian Security Team Headquarters reported the other day that villagers in Xikou reported that there was a large band of local bandits in Wangjiashan, behind Houjiangshan, about fifty or sixty people, led by Wu A’gen, and they had a large number of new-style firearms. The residents near the mountain were all surrounded and in great danger, and they requested that they be suppressed. After receiving the report, the head of the team, Mao Tinghui, made arrangements to send troops to pursue and suppress them.

Village Head Sun Guiqing Sentenced to Imprisonment: Sun Guiqing, the former village head of Xinlu Village in the Taiqiu District of Zhenhai, was sued by Dai Shengding and others for encroaching on public bonds and public funds. The case was summoned by the county judge Cai Cheng to the court to hear both parties. At the end of the debate, Guiqing was sentenced to four years and three months in prison for the crime of encroaching on public funds.

Qu County

The County Magistrate and Chief of Public Security Bureau Take Their Oaths of Office: Since taking office, Wu Bokang, the magistrate of Qu County, has made many reforms to county administration, and local sentiments are quite harmonious. It is reported that at 9 a.m. on August 12, a supplementary oath of office ceremony was held in the county government memorial hall. The province has telegraphed the county party headquarters to send personnel to supervise the oath.
