People from all walks of life attended, which was very grand.

Anqing

General Order to Survey and Report on Autumn Harvest: The Anhui Provincial Department of Civil Affairs and Department of Finance stated that since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been favorable, and the crops in various places have grown vigorously. However, after the start of summer, there has been excessive continuous rain, and many embankments along the Yangtze River and Huai River have collapsed. Although low-lying fields have been flooded, higher-lying fields and hilly fields have not been flooded and can be expected to yield a bumper harvest. Yesterday, a joint general order was issued to sixty counties that the county magistrate should personally conduct a thorough survey of all cases of disaster reporting and insurance claims, and submit detailed reports.

Guangfeng Embankment Collapses, Emergency Relief to Be Issued: The Guangfeng embankment in Badu Lake, Dongliu, fifteen li across the river from Anqing, has approximately 100,000 mu of farmland and a population of approximately tens of thousands. Its annual output is worth approximately one million yuan. Recently, due to the rising floodwaters, the embankment has repeatedly reported dangers. Officials and gentry have tried their best to rescue it for many days. At 4 p.m. on the 10th, the embankment near Mashiqiao collapsed due to strong winds and waves, killing more than 400 embankment workers who fell into the water. The residents fled to Badushan and set fire to their houses to provide light. After receiving the report, the Department of Civil Affairs forwarded it to the provincial government to allocate emergency relief, dispatch teams to maintain order, and telegraph Yang Yingzhi, the magistrate of Dongliu County, to quickly comfort the victims and strictly prevent rioters from inciting trouble.

Page 13

Local News

Flood Disaster

Relief Committee

National Government Promulgates

Responsible for Preparing Relief

The National News Agency reports that yesterday, the National Government promulgated the establishment of the National Government Flood Relief Committee to handle the relief efforts for the unprecedented flood in the Yangtze River basin and other areas. The government is deeply aware of the breadth and severity of this disaster, which is unprecedented in China in the past century. Therefore, it is making every effort to grant the committee the highest authority to cooperate with various relief agencies in the country in order to achieve the goal of providing relief to tens of millions of disaster victims.

Special Commissioners: The government has recently appointed Song Ziwen, Vice President of the Executive Yuan, Liu Shangqing, Minister of Interior, Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Industry, Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Relief Committee, and Zhu Qinglan, who is responsible for relief efforts in the Northwest, as members of the committee, and Song, the Vice President of the Executive Yuan, as the chairman. In the coming days, more enthusiastic people from China and abroad will be selected as members.

The Headquarters is Located in Shanghai: The headquarters is temporarily located next to the Central Bank at No. 1 Jiujiang Road in Shanghai. Zeng Rongpu has been appointed as the secretary-general of the committee. The Chinese telegraph code for the committee is 2182, and the English code is Floodrel.

Cooperate Together: According to the person in charge of the committee, this committee is not limited to government personnel, and it is planned to invite charitable people from all walks of life across the country to cooperate together. There are many Chinese and foreign organizations and individuals who have expressed their willingness to join and assist, and the government is very grateful. The committee also attaches great importance to private relief organizations, and does not want the establishment of this committee by the government to cause the progress of various relief efforts to be slackened. A special department will be set up in the committee to facilitate contact with various charitable organizations and carry out relief efforts.

Assist in Investigation: According to reports from various places, it is sufficient to prove that the disaster is serious, but the detailed situation is still difficult to understand. Therefore, the committee plans to conduct a detailed investigation immediately, with river engineering experts and engineers flying to the disaster area by plane to conduct measurements, and requesting customs, postal, and telegraph agencies to report accurately at any time. In addition to the investigation reports from local authorities in the disaster-stricken provinces and regions, the committee has also entrusted Chinese and foreign private organizations, such as the Bank of China, the Flour Association, Standard Oil, British American Tobacco, and churches in various places, to assist in investigating the conditions in the disaster area in order to clarify the truth.

Organization of the Committee: Although the committee was established yesterday, the related personnel have already made plans for the organization. The committee will set up seven sections: the Investigation Section, the Finance Section, the Accounting and Auditing Section, the Health and Epidemic Prevention Section, the Transportation Section, the Disaster Area Work Section, and the Liaison Section. Baker, an advisor to the Ministry of Railways, has handled disaster relief in North China many times and has now been transferred by the committee.

Disaster Area Work: A continuous plan will be implemented within a few months. Due to the massive scale of this flood, with the crops of tens of millions of farmers submerged and agricultural implements washed away, relief should be provided. Until the end of spring next year, after the water recedes, it is planned to have farmers replant vegetables and winter wheat that can be harvested in winter. The committee also plans to use work as relief, allowing disaster victims to engage in repairing embankments, cleaning up disaster areas, building roads, etc. A large number of experienced engineering personnel have been recruited from various parties for this purpose.

This flood has caused great harm. The government knows that it is not like the partial disasters in previous years in various provinces, which could be handled simply by distributing a small amount of money and by local and private relief organizations. The Yangtze River basin is the area of China's wealth, and for the sake of protecting the foundation of the country, the government's relief plan will not only provide food and clothing for the disaster victims in various places, but will also enable the areas to restore their local production capacity.

Wang Zhengting's Remarks

Japanese Sailors Arresting People in the Huangpu River

Handled by the Municipal Government

Three Protests Regarding the Korean Issue Yet to Be Issued

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting arrived in Shanghai by train from Nanjing at 10:40 last night. A reporter from this newspaper interviewed him on the train. According to Foreign Minister Wang, he only saw reports about the incident of Japanese sailors assaulting and arresting anti-Japanese association inspectors in the Huangpu River in the newspapers. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not yet received a formal report. The matter is currently being handled by the municipal government with the Japanese side. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs will handle it after receiving a detailed report from the municipal government. As for the Japanese side's second response to the Korean issue, it cannot be released until both parties agree. Our country's third protest is still under consideration and is expected to be sent out in the near future. In addition, the credentials of Ambassador to Japan Jiang Zuobin need to be signed by Chairman Jiang, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has sent them to Jiangxi by airmail for Chairman Jiang to sign. It is expected to arrive soon. Ambassador Jiang will go to Japan after receiving his credentials. The credentials of the Japanese Ambassador Mamoru Shigemitsu will be presented after Chairman Jiang returns to Nanjing. At present, all negotiations can still proceed as usual, as this is international practice. It does not matter if the credentials are delivered half a year later.

Japanese Sailors Abducting People and Robbing Goods

The Municipal Government Lodged a Protest Yesterday

Strong Statements from the Party Headquarters and Labor Unions

On the evening of the 12th of this month, anti-Japanese association inspectors were beaten by Japanese sailors for detaining Japanese goods and were imprisoned in the Japanese Consulate General. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau sent personnel to negotiate their release, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that Mayor Zhang believes that the Japanese Navy's actions of assault and robbery violate international law and disregard our country's sovereignty. Yesterday, he lodged the most serious protest with the Japanese Consul General in Shanghai, Kuramatsu Murai. At the same time, party headquarters in various districts, labor unions, and the municipal federation have all made very strong statements. Details are as follows:

Mayor Zhang's Letter to the Japanese Consul: I am writing to you regarding the report that on the evening of the 12th of this month, four Chinese people were abducted by armed Japanese soldiers on the Huangpu River in this city. They were violently beaten and injured and then imprisoned in your consulate. The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent personnel to negotiate their release. The fact that Japanese naval soldiers abducted Chinese people within Chinese territory and that your consulate detained these people is a disregard for our country's sovereignty and a violation of international law. The incident occurred because these people were holding a mass movement. All their measures should only be subject to Chinese law. Even if there are any careless actions, it is certainly not for your country's authorities to directly interfere. If such illegal actions were to incite an incident, who would be responsible? Based on the aforementioned, I, the mayor, lodge the most serious protest and request that you investigate and severely punish the soldiers who caused the incident, compensate the injured Chinese people, guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future, and express your apology to maintain good relations and avoid disputes. I hope to receive a reply.

Declaration of the Third District Party Headquarters: (Titles omitted) The report that Japanese soldiers forcibly seized sacks and detained and beat inspectors of the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association in our country is shocking. Japan, with its small island nation, suffers from overpopulation and actively seeks external development. Our Chinese nation is its only target. The tragedies of "May Fourth," "May Ninth," "May Thirtieth," and "May Third" clearly demonstrate this. The entire national humiliation history of the Chinese nation was created by Japanese imperialism. This time, due to the Wanbaoshan Incident, they incited Korean people to massacre overseas Chinese, resulting in numerous deaths and inhumane atrocities. All circles in this city, saddened by the impending national crisis and the approaching doomsday, strive for survival and dare not slacken. Hence, the organization of the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee was formed to carry out economic severance with Japan in a determined and courageous spirit. This has aroused suspicion from Japanese imperialism, which has spared no despicable means to sabotage it in every possible way. They even forcibly seized confiscated inferior goods and arrested anti-Japanese personnel in our country, subjecting them to various forms of violence, even to the point of disappearance. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? However, it is found that the occurrence of such unfortunate events is due to cold-blooded merchants who covet petty profits and do not hesitate to use the force of Japanese soldiers to protect them. Therefore, this association dares to contribute its views: (1) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs should be urged to negotiate with Japan as soon as possible to achieve the goals of punishing the perpetrators, apologizing, compensating, guaranteeing, and withdrawing Japanese warships stationed in China. (2) The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association should offer rewards and publish announcements to expose merchants who purchase sacks from the Dongya Factory and transport large quantities of Japanese goods. Once verified, they will be severely punished with the force of the masses to deter traitors. In addition to petitioning superiors to implement the aforementioned proposals, this association will lead its members to expand publicity and urge the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association to continue its struggle. It is hoped that all compatriots will unanimously advocate that the entire Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese movement will not be ruined by a few merchants or succumb to the violence of Japanese imperialism. This is deeply fortunate. Chinese Kuomintang Shanghai Special City Third District Executive Committee. In addition, the Ninth and Thirtieth Sub-branches of the Third District and the Third Sub-branch of the Eighth District have all issued declarations, the text of which is omitted.

Telegram from the Eighth District Party Headquarters: The Eighth District Party Headquarters telegrams to all newspapers in Shanghai for the attention of all compatriots: Unfortunately, our country is suffering from repeated foreign invasions. Japanese imperialists are extremely fierce and regard our country as meat on the chopping board and treat the Eastern Provinces as colonies to be nibbled away. Their ambition is growing daily. They destroyed our good men and slaughtered our farmers in the Wanbaoshan area and incited hooligans in Korea to attack and beat people at will. All areas where our overseas Chinese merchants live and work have been destroyed. Within ten days, thousands of people have died, and the number of injured is countless, creating a terrifying situation. However, Japanese imperialists have no intention of repenting. Recently, Japanese warships stationed in Shanghai have repeatedly sent armed sailors to invade the Chinese territory, robbing goods, arresting compatriots, and brutally beating officials of the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association. Their sinister intentions are evident. If we do not take immediate action to deal with this trampling of our nation and disregard for our country's rights, what can we expect for the future? It is hoped that our countrymen will rise up and pursue the matter directly, insist on reason and strive for it, and fight Japanese imperialism to the end to wipe out this great shame, strive for the survival of the nation, and strive for the survival of the country. We send this urgent telegram with extreme excitement and indignation. Chinese Kuomintang Shanghai Special City Eighth District Party Headquarters.

Declaration of the Ninth District Party Headquarters: The boycott of Japanese goods is purely a manifestation of the patriotic psychology of our people. Confiscating inferior goods is a necessary means to implement economic severance. No one can prevent it. However, Japanese imperialists did not immediately wake up and stop their policy of aggression against China. Instead, in Shanghai, a major transportation hub, when our patriotic action confiscated Japanese goods, they used force to rob goods, kidnapped four inspectors, and brutally beat them, leaving them covered in blood. The shocking news has been spread, and we cannot help but be furious. Thinking back, the old shame of May 30th has not yet been avenged, and the Wanbaoshan incident has occurred again. Now, the brutal and tyrannical Japanese imperialists want to repeat the tragedy in Shanghai and spill blood on Nanjing Road. It must be known that the people under the banner of the Three People's Principles revolution have a spirit of great fearlessness and will never be subdued by force. They are not afraid of the trampling of iron hooves or the sweeping of bullets. They would rather build a city with white bones to protect our beautiful rivers and mountains and sprinkle blood on the ground to seek the freedom of our nation. In addition to sending a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association to step up its work, this association is willing to have all comrades and compatriots in the country follow the precepts of the rise and fall of the world and the responsibility of every citizen, rise up together, boycott Japanese goods, make persistent efforts, and carry it through to the end.

Declarations of Various Labor Unions: Shanghai Municipal Labor Unions solemnly declare against the barbarous acts of Japanese soldiers abducting and robbing. Central Party Headquarters, National Government, Party Headquarters at all levels, governments of all provinces, cities, and counties, labor unions, mass organizations, newspapers, all attention: Since the Japanese used the Wanbaoshan incident to incite Korean people to massacre overseas Chinese, their insidious intentions and outrageous atrocities have been exposed to the world. All those with blood and qi cannot but be angry. Our government, in the midst of the Japanese's increasingly aggressive atrocities, is willing to endure humiliation and still believes that the Japanese can be reasoned with and that world peace must be maintained. Therefore, on the one hand, it lodges a protest and still treats the Japanese with sincerity and openness in accordance with international etiquette. On the other hand, it publishes the facts to the international nations to clarify the truth and uphold justice. At the same time, it automatically raises funds to provide relief to the overseas Chinese who have suffered, hoping that the Japanese will lay down their butcher knives and take the opportunity to pull back from the brink and achieve a good outcome. The intention of our national government can be said to be perfect. However, the Japanese are still stubborn and unrepentant, perfunctorily and evasively dealing with repeated protests, exhausting their cunning and insidious abilities. Gradually, the overseas Chinese in the areas where the tragedy occurred have nowhere to bury the dead and no way to escape. Disturbances by mobs still occur anytime and anywhere, and crises are everywhere, but the Japanese turn a blind eye. Not only that, but our compatriots, hating the barbarity of the Japanese, unanimously declared economic severance with Japan in a determined and courageous spirit to urge them to repent. Unexpectedly, the Japanese imperialists have no intention of repenting and dare to intensify their actions. On the 11th of this month, the Japanese imperialists repeatedly dispatched Japanese soldiers with guns and live ammunition to the Suzhou Creek and Huangpu River areas in Shanghai to forcibly rob the Japanese goods seized by the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association organized by our people from all walks of life. They also abducted five officials of the association. After four of them were released, they were covered in injuries and treated like prisoners. The whereabouts of one person are unknown. Is their despicable behavior and barbaric methods not a disregard for international law and the civilization of demons and a common enemy of mankind? Our 400 million compatriots, in this time of national crisis, only have one choice: to rise up together and fight them to the last victory. Survival is at stake. We will go through fire and water and will not hesitate. At the same time, we also hope that all sectors of society across the country will work together to organize the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association, adhere to the economic severance with Japan, and control this evil. We will make thorough plans to help the overseas Chinese in distress, without distinguishing between regions or boundaries, with one heart and one mind, from beginning to end. Our associations and others will serve the country and will not hesitate to move forward and attack without falling behind, and we will eventually bury the giant barbarians to maintain our peace, and then we will be satisfied. At this time of crisis, if there are those who flatter foreigners and are greedy, disregard the national difficulties, and have ulterior motives to sabotage the organization of the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association, then they are close to treason, and this association will use the same methods to deal with them as it does with imperialists, so that the river will be clear and the anti-Japanese work, the welfare of the overseas Chinese, and the national status can all advance without limits. Words cannot express our intentions, but we hope you will take it to heart. This declaration is made by the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, the Publishing Industry Union, the Water and Electricity Industry Unions in various districts, the Cotton Textile Industry Unions in various districts, the Cigarette Industry Unions in various districts, the Pharmaceutical Industry Union, the Bookbinding Industry Union, the Ship Timber Industry Union, and more than one hundred other labor unions on August 14th.

In addition, the Shanghai Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union, Shipbuilding Industry Union, Paper Industry Union, Loading and Unloading Industry Union, Match Industry Union, Bottle Industry Union, Water and Wood Industry Union, Garment Industry Union, Country Wine Production Industry Union, Basket Carrier Industry Union, Coarse Cloth Industry Union, and Civil Ship Repair Industry Union have sent telegrams, the text of which is omitted.

Telegram from the Municipal Federation: The Municipal Federation's telegram regarding the barbarity of the Japanese soldiers is directed to the Nanjing National Government, the Ministry of the Navy, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Songhu Garrison Headquarters: On August 13th at 1:00 AM, the Japanese Naval Office, now stationed on the Anzhai warship in Shanghai, sent 25 armed sailors on a small steamer to invade Lujiazui, the inland area of Shanghai, robbing goods waiting to be checked and released and abducting the cargo inspectors. Except for the four who were released after negotiation, the whereabouts of one person are unknown. After this case occurred, all citizens were shocked and indignant. Everyone felt that the Japanese were behaving in an uncivilized and brutal manner, which was beyond words. It can be inferred that in their eyes, there is no China, so they dare to wield their weapons at night and enter the area where Chinese military police are stationed as if it were no man's land. Robbing goods and abducting people and leaving safely is like taking something out of a pocket. In this situation, it is difficult for the Chinese military police to avoid responsibility for lax defense, but the actions of the Japanese soldiers are no different from those of robbers. Human sentiment and legal principles are not tolerated. How can neighboring friendly nations do this? In this case, the Ministry of the Navy should order the warship to disarm the Anzhai warship and order it to leave the country. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs should also lodge a strong protest and severely punish the commanding officers of the Japanese Naval Office, return the one cargo inspector whose whereabouts are unknown by a set deadline, and punish the perpetrators, apologize, compensate, and guarantee that there will be no similar riots in the future. The Songhu Garrison Headquarters and the Municipal Government should also strictly order their subordinate military police to strictly defend and not allow armed foreign bandits to invade the country at will. If foreign bandits invade, they should be disarmed immediately and sent to the ministry for investigation. Only in this way can the country's rights be protected and security and aftermath be maintained. This telegram is sent to you with utmost sincerity. Shanghai Special Zone Citizens' Federation.

New Stamp Design and Colors

To Be Issued Early Next Month

The Postal Administration of the Ministry of Communications previously ordered 150 million National Revolutionary Party Founder Sun Yat-sen stamps from the British De La Rue Printing Company, with a five-year term, to be printed and delivered to the Administration annually. The first batch of 120 million stamps has been shipped to Shanghai, divided into denominations of 1 fen, 2 fen, 4 fen, and 2 jiao. The 2 jiao stamp is blue, the 4 fen stamp is light green, the 2 fen stamp is green, and the 1 fen stamp is golden yellow. All of them feature a portrait of the National Revolutionary Party Founder Sun Yat-sen and the Blue Sky with a White Sun. The size is the same as that of the old-style stamps. The Postal Administration has now reported to the Ministry of Communications, and it has been decided internally that from September 1st, postal districts in all provinces will implement their use. It has been decided that the old-style stamps will no longer be printed. After they are used up, they will be replaced with the new stamps. There are also seven other types of new stamps engraved with the portraits of Huang Xing, Song Jiaoren, Chen Qimei, Deng Keng, etc., which were contracted to the Beiping Ministry of Finance Printing Bureau for printing. They have not yet been printed, so they cannot be used at the same time. As for the four types of new Sun Yat-sen stamps, a way was found to make printing plates and publish them first, so that the general public and stamp collectors can see them first.

At the Same Time, Receiving Various Departments and Associations from the Previous Session

Yesterday Morning

Noulens and His Wife Escorted to Nanjing

Swiss Consulate Confirms Noulens Is Not a Swiss National

The Da Mei Evening News reports that the important Communist Party member, the Westerner Noulens, and his wife were escorted to Nanjing by the Garrison Headquarters this morning (the 14th) and will be tried in a military court in Nanjing. The Swiss Consulate General has also confirmed that Noulens is not a Swiss national. It was learned from this port today that after the arrest of the two and the discovery of important documents, dozens of Communist suspects have been arrested in Java, the Indian Ocean colonies, and the Philippines, including many foreigners. Chinese authorities have also received reports that Noulens and his wife held important positions in the Moscow Soviet Committee. Although the authorities are not yet willing to make any announcements regarding this case, it is expected that after studying the case documents, they will know the activities of the Communist Party in Shanghai and will continue to make arrests. It is reported that Noulens' deputy, a Westerner, has secretly left Shanghai and fled elsewhere. When Noulens and his wife were escorted to the train this morning, they were guarded by armed soldiers. After the group got out of the car, Mrs. Noulens walked through the platform with her head down and entered the train without looking around. Her face showed sadness. Her husband looked around from time to time, still with a hint of hope. In the train, the two sat about ten feet apart and spoke in German from time to time.

Genuine Invoices and Fake Invoices

Unscrupulous Merchants Falsely Impersonating Japanese Merchants to Transport Goods

The Anti-Japanese Association Finds Genuine Evidence

On the 10th of this month, inspectors from the Zhabei District Inspection Office of the Anti-Japanese Association, including Inspector Yin Jianxia, ​​confiscated two carts of various glass bottles on Xibaoxing Road. However, the deliveryman insisted that the glass bottles were sold by the Baocheng Glass Factory to the Japanese merchants Dongjin and Jinxing Foreign Companies and not to Chinese businesses. He also took out two invoices from Dongjin and Jinxing as proof and requested to be released. However, the inspection office had previously received a tip that there were genuine invoices hidden on the deliveryman's body and that the invoices taken out as proof were deliberately faked in the name of Japanese merchants. The inspectors immediately carried out an inspection and finally found a genuine invoice from the Baocheng Glass Factory to the Xie Shang Company on the deliveryman's body, which listed the names and quantities of the goods and was exactly the same as the one falsely made in the name of Dongjin. It was clear that he had deliberately made a fake invoice to deceive the port. The goods were all confiscated and the genuine and fake invoices were sent to the Anti-Japanese Association for thorough investigation.

Anti-Japanese Association News

Collecting Funds for Necessities

Returning Confiscated Goods on a Scheduled Basis

The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee's economic severance with Japan this time, according to the decided plan, on the one hand, strictly confiscates goods in a revolutionary manner, and on the other hand, actively promotes production in a constructive plan, with the goal of achieving thorough boycott. The confiscation of goods has been very successful in the north and south of the city, as well as in Pudong and Huxi. Although there have been setbacks, we will not slacken. In terms of production, in addition to estimating that Li Quanshi, Xu Yongzuo, and Gui Yanfang are drafting a five-year plan, a considerable decision has been made on the method of collecting industrial funds from various industries. The details are as follows:

Decision to Collect Funds: The principle of collecting industrial funds was passed at the fifth executive committee meeting, and Zheng Chengqing, Lu Xingzhuang, Yan Esheng, Wang Yansong, Hu Fengxiang, and others were appointed to draft detailed measures. At the same time, the Design Committee also submitted a proposal. The sixth executive committee meeting was held at 5:00 PM the day before yesterday to discuss and decide on the following cases: (1) For industrial raw material necessities, each industry should automatically organize raw material factories within two months and extract industrial funds. The funds will be used as factory shares in the future. Before the factories are established, if the industry unions request the association and the association verifies that it is true, they will be temporarily issued permits, but industrial funds must be collected. (2) Before the methods for each case are decided, the funds will be temporarily collected at one-tenth of the price of the goods. (3) Yarn fund: According to the request of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Dyeing and Weaving Joint Association, (A) five taels (B) seven and a half taels of two types. It has now been decided to change to (A) seven and a half taels (B) ten taels of two types. (4) The three committee members Tao Baichuan, Zhang Honghai, and Chen Songyuan will review the general rules for the collection and safekeeping of industrial funds.

Releasing Confiscated Goods: According to the steps for disposing of Japanese goods stipulated by the Anti-Japanese Association, all confiscated goods, after verification: (1) If the payment was made before July 14th, a relief fund equivalent to 10% of the price of the goods should be paid; (2) If the payment was made after July 14th and before July 24th, a relief fund equivalent to 20% of the price of the goods should be paid; (3) If the payment was made after July 24th, all will be confiscated. Now that the registration deadline has passed, the sixth executive committee meeting also discussed and decided on all goods that have been confiscated and are being re-registered: (1) The registration department should submit the registration forms for confiscated Japanese goods to the investigation department before the 15th of this month; (2) The investigation department should check the goods according to the registration forms to see if they match and report to the standing committee before the 19th of this month; (3) From the 20th of this month, the owners of the goods can pay the relief fund and receive the certificate to return the confiscated goods.

Continued Confiscation of Japanese Goods: The association's inspection department released the eleventh, twelfth, and thirteenth confiscation reports: (1) Eleventh report: August 10th, four bundles of Yitai thread, two bundles of Nan Gongyi coal shovels, ten boxes of Yong Da Xiang Yaoji sundries, one burlap sack, one bundle of foreign umbrellas, August 11th, one piece of Feng Da Zhixu at Feijia Ferry, twenty pieces of Xie Xing Company soy sauce, and thirty-one pieces of Yuan Xiang lead wire; (2) Twelfth report: August 11th, twenty-six bags of Wufeng white powder outside Xiaodongmen, one package of dried shrimp from the Pinghu Shipping Bureau at the Dada Wharf, and seven small boxes of Baotai glass at the Dali Wharf; (3) Thirteenth report: August 11th, three pieces of sugar from the Gong Mao Shipping Bureau on Maigen Road, August 12th, one box of Quan Changlong tooth powder and one box of sundries at the Xinbeimen, one hundred and twenty-eight packages of dried kelp from Zhu Sanbao at the Hongsheng Wharf in Pudong, one hundred packages of Zilaihuo stalks from Zhang Xiaoshen at the Shuntai Wharf, forty pieces of matchbox sheets and thirty boxes of ammonium sulfide at the Waibaidu Bridge.

Minutes of the Standing Committee Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Goods Research Association

Resolution: Strictly Boycott Luxury and General Goods

Collect Funds for Essential Goods and Industrial Raw Materials

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's Anti-Japanese Goods Research Committee held a standing committee meeting at 2 PM yesterday in the standing committee room of the Chamber of Commerce. Committee members Zheng Chengqing, Yang Housheng, Ye Chunqiao, Ye Jiaxing, Zheng Zenan, Lu Qisheng, and others (totaling seven members) attended, with Zheng Chengqing chairing and Jin Shengbai recording. The following resolutions were made: (A) Reporting Matters: (1) The previous plenary meeting resolved to assign tasks to each committee for group work, which has been carried out accordingly. (2) At the same meeting, the sugar industry requested the establishment of domestic sugar factories, and the resolution to forward it to the Chamber of Commerce has been implemented, and it has been resolved by the Chamber of Commerce's standing committee and submitted. (B) Discussion Matters: (1) Regarding the scheduling of the Standing Committee meeting, it was resolved to hold it every Friday at 1 PM. (2) Regarding the procedures for each group, it was resolved that all cases submitted for research should be assigned by the standing committee members, based on their nature, to the heads of each group for research. After completion of the research, each group should provide written opinions and submit them to the Standing Committee for review. (3) Discussion of Hu Jiqian's letter suggesting methods for boycotting goods: It was resolved to file the case and reply to the letter accepting the suggestion. (4) Discussion of He Bomao's letter suggesting methods for boycotting goods: It was resolved to forward it to the Anti-Japanese Association and reply to Mr. He. (5) Discussion of the letter from the Electrical Silk Velvet Industry Association regarding the lack of domestic substitutes for 60-count yarn, requesting assistance. (6) Two letters from the Changshu County Chamber of Commerce, one concerning the essential raw materials for textile factories and the other concerning the need for flexibility in shipping before adequate self-sufficiency is achieved, it was resolved to reply that they should be handled in accordance with the resolutions of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association. (7) Discussion of the letter from the Coal Industry Association regarding the proposed fundraising for an enterprise fund and the submission of an outline for record-keeping: It was resolved to approve it in principle and forward the original proposal to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce for review. (8) Discussion of how to distribute the cases that have been resolved by the first plenary meeting and assigned to each group for handling: It was resolved that the Chairman should review and issue the files. (C) Provisional Proposals: (1) Discussion of the date for the first group meetings of each group: It was resolved that the Luxury Goods Group and the Essential Goods Group should meet next Monday, and the General Goods Group and the Industrial Raw Materials Group should meet next Tuesday, convened by the heads of each group. (2) Discussion of determining research principles: It was resolved: (1) For luxury goods and general goods, the principle should be strict boycotting, and the detailed classification should be researched by each group. (2) For essential goods and industrial raw materials, funds should be collected, with the standard for industrial raw materials being 5% to 10% of the value, and for essential goods being 10% to 20% of the value. The detailed classification and collection levels should be researched by each group.

New Canadian Tariff on Chinese Goods

Increased for All Goods, Except a Slight Reduction for Tea

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday issued a directive to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stating that the ministry had received a notification from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs based on a report from the Consulate General in Canada, that the Canadian Parliament had passed a budget bill which included the following items related to China: (1) All imported goods, whether duty-free or taxable, are subject to a special tax of 1% ad valorem. (2) The import tariffs have been revised, and the following items have an impact on Chinese goods imported into Canada: (A) Canned fruits, formerly taxed at US$0.03 per pound, are now increased to US$0.05. (B) Corn, formerly duty-free, is now subject to a tax of CAD$0.25 per bushel. (C) Rice, formerly taxed at US$0.75 per 100 pounds, is now increased to CAD$1.00. (D) Tea, formerly taxed at US$0.10 per pound, is now reduced to US$0.08. (E) Wood products, formerly taxed at 30%, are now increased to 45%. A survey form of tariffs on Chinese goods imported into Canada, filled out by this consulate, is submitted for your review, etc. The information reported by the Consulate General has considerable reference value. In addition to replying to the Ministry, this order is issued for your information. This order.

The Chilean Embassy Temporarily Establishes an Office

Located in the Cathay Hotel on the Bund

The newly appointed Chargé d'Affaires of Chile to China, Mr. Blanco Sierra, after arriving in Shanghai, once went to Beijing to pay respects to the Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Zhengting and various important figures of the National Government. After returning to Shanghai, he prepared to establish an office of the embassy in Shanghai. However, in recent times, Mr. Blanco found it quite difficult to find a suitable building. Therefore, for the convenience of office work, he has decided to first establish a temporary office in the Cathay Hotel on the Bund and has hired Feng Tianying, a special Shanghai-based reporter from the French "Political News" in Peiping, as his secretary. Mr. Feng graduated from the University of Lyon in France and previously served as a secretary at the Turkish Embassy. The temporary office has already begun operating, with hours temporarily set from 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM. However, formal notifications have not yet been sent to various Chinese and foreign agencies and organizations, and it is expected that a notification will be sent after a permanent embassy is found. At that time, negotiations on the new Sino-Chilean treaty will also commence.

Current whereabouts of prominent figures

Chen Shaokuan returned to Beijing by overnight train from Shanghai yesterday.

Lian Shenghai and Wang Boqun arrived in Shanghai by overnight train from Beijing yesterday.

French Concession Tram Restarts Yesterday

Conflict between Car Department and Mechanical Department, Guaranteed by Du Yuesheng

However, Temporary Short-Term Workers' Demands Unresolved

Social Affairs Bureau Inquired About 8-Hour Workday

Today, the Labor Union Holds a Victory Meeting at Zhuangyuanlou

French Concession power and tram workers officially resumed work yesterday, restoring all routes to their original state. The car department is awaiting a response from the company, and all workers are demanding an eight-hour workday, creating a rather serious situation. Short-term workers are still on strike due to unresolved demands for improved treatment. The labor union is holding a victory celebration today. The details of each situation are recorded below:

Please Du Yuesheng for Guarantee: The Third District Power and Tram Industry Union held a joint meeting of directors and supervisors at 5 PM the day before yesterday, chaired by Xu Yushu. After receiving a secret report that the car department workers were going to pick a fight with the mechanical department workers, the meeting decided to send representatives Lu Guanhong, Zhang Renjun, Zhang Amao, Zhu Along, Zhang Yinsheng, and Qiao Linggen to Du Yuesheng's private residence at 7 PM to request a guarantee. Du Yuesheng agreed to be responsible for the guarantee, hoping that everyone would work in peace.

All Cars Fully Restored: Starting yesterday, more than 800 employees in the car department, including ticket sellers, drivers, ticket inspectors, and ticket clerks, officially resumed work. Tram routes 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, and 60, trolley routes 17 and 18, and bus routes 21 and 22 are all operating as normal. On that day, over 80 trams, over 20 trolley buses, and 18 buses were dispatched. As for the car department's proposed requests for a published apology and punishment of the perpetrators, the company is still considering them. The car department has stated that they are awaiting a response.

Labor-Management Consultation: Over 200 temporary short-term workers at the French Concession Power and Tram Company requested (1) a 30% increase in wages for each person per day, (2) a minimum employment period of eight months, and (3) full pay on Sundays, but these were not granted. As a result, they went on strike on the afternoon of the 12th and sent representatives to ask Chinese Director Du Yuesheng to negotiate with the company manager, Monsalut. The result was that the company only agreed to an increase of five cents per person per day, which was not resolved. Yesterday, they again asked Du Yuesheng to negotiate with the manager. The manager only agreed to (1) continue to increase wages by five cents per person per day and (2) one day off for every six days worked, refusing to agree to anything else. The workers insisted that the minimum employment period be six months, so it remained unresolved. Negotiations will continue today, and it is expected that the issue will be resolved, and the strike will not escalate.

Negotiations on Working Hours: The Second District Electric Workers' Union received a response from the company manager, Monsalut, agreeing to respond before August 18. Yesterday, the union sent another letter to the company, stating: "To Whom It May Concern: After investigating the implementation of the Factory Law by the National Government since August 1, all major factories in Shanghai and the Municipal Council have implemented it. However, your company has delayed implementing the provisions of Article 8 of Chapter 3 of the law, which establishes an eight-hour workday as a principle. We do not know why. After deliberation by the joint meeting of directors and supervisors, we request that your company quickly implement an eight-hour workday to comply with the law and avoid disputes."

Inquiry by the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs: After receiving a request from the labor union to implement an eight-hour workday, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs summoned everyone for questioning on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Xu A-mei, the chairman of the Second District Electric Industry Union, and Zhang Zhenyuan, the chairman of the Bureau of Social Affairs, attended. The labor representatives stated (1) that Article 8 of the Factory Law stipulates that the actual working hours for adult workers should be eight hours per day in principle, and (2) that the French Municipal Council has already implemented an eight-hour workday. The chairman announced the end of the questioning and rescheduled to conduct mediation.

Labor Union Victory Celebration: The Second District Power and Tram Industry Union, formerly the French Concession Power and Tram Union, will hold a victory celebration at Zhuangyuanlou in Baxianqiao at 7 PM today to celebrate the reinstatement of Xu A-mei and 27 others who were previously dismissed. All sectors are invited to participate. Chinese Director Du Yuesheng has also agreed to send police to maintain order at that time. It is said that Zhuangyuanlou is already setting up a decorated archway.

Local News II

Fulu Li Road

Counterfeit Money Ring Broken

Privately Manufacturing Counterfeit Notes from Various Banks

Totaling Tens of Thousands of Dollars

French Concession Detectives Investigate

French Concession detectives Tao Desheng, Wang Zhihao, Chen Yishan, and Qi Deqing learned the day before yesterday that someone had privately set up a counterfeit money manufacturing operation at No. 46, Jianye Li, Fulu Li Road in the French Concession. They went to the location quietly and confiscated counterfeit banknotes totaling $1,420, including 294 five-dollar notes, 36 ten-dollar notes, 42 five-dollar notes, 392 half-dollar notes, 98 five-dollar notes, 599 five-dollar notes, and one five-dollar note from various banks, as well as two manufacturing machines. They arrested nine individuals including Gu Jinsheng, Gu Gengsheng, Wu Jinsheng, Yao Yiqing, Wang Rongsheng, Li Rufei, Zhang Aliu, and women Gu Wangshi and Ye Chenshi, and brought them to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the Second Special District Court for investigation. First, police attorney Gu Shouxi stated that the case was broken because Zhang Aliu used a five-dollar counterfeit note to buy a dollar's worth of soap at a store opened by a Westerner named Byro at 655 Avenue Joffre, and Byro noticed it and reported it to the police. The detectives then successively solved the case. It was found that the defendants in this case counterfeited these banknotes in the amount of tens of thousands of dollars and sent people to distribute them. The main culprits are still at large, so please issue warrants to arrest them for interrogation. Judge Xiong questioned each defendant briefly and then ordered them to be detained and rescheduled for further questioning.

"Weisheng" Steamship

Shipwrecked Crew and Passengers Arrive in Shanghai

The "Weisheng" steamship of Jardine Matheson was wrecked off the coast of Wenzhou due to the severe storm, which has already been reported in this newspaper. The shipwrecked crew and passengers have now arrived in Shanghai on a Guangdong steamship. Further details are reported below:

"Weisheng" Aground on Reef: The "Weisheng" steamship was en route from Hong Kong to Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 9th, when it arrived at Nanguan Bay off the coast of Wenzhou, the captain, Mr. Hsu, observed the weather and knew that a strong storm was coming. He steered the ship into the Nanguan Bay Strait to shelter from the storm. That night, two anchors were dropped. There was no damage to the ship. By 8:00 AM on the 10th, the wind had increased, and the ship was driven aground by the storm. The bottom of the ship was punctured. Although cargo on the deck was thrown into the sea, it was still unavoidable. According to the captain of the Guangdong steamship, the "Weisheng" steamship is still aground on the reef, listing to one side, and all cabins have been flooded.

Crew and Passengers Rescued to Shanghai: At the beginning of the "Weisheng" shipwreck, the captain immediately launched lifeboats to transport the passengers ashore for temporary shelter. The first boat launched was smashed on a reef by the wind. At that time, the radio was broken. Fortunately, there was still a spare machine that could send out a distress signal, but it could not reach far. The Tai Koo's Guangdong steamship received the signal, which was about 100 nautical miles from Nanguan Bay, and immediately relayed it to Hong Kong and Shanghai and sailed to rescue them. It was not until the morning of the 11th that it was able to enter the bay and rescued 43 passengers and crew members from the "Weisheng" steamship, carrying them to Shanghai, where they have now arrived.

Rescue Ships and Warships Rush to the Scene: After receiving the telegram, Jardine Matheson first sent the "Hengsheng" steamship, and then telegraphed Japan to send a salvage ship. It should arrive in Hong Kong today. The British Navy also dispatched the destroyer HMS Spey to protect them. The "Hengsheng" steamship is currently guarding outside the "Weisheng." Yesterday, the Hong Kong-based "Hesheng" and "Dangsheng" steamships were dispatched to the shipwreck site to assist in the rescue.

Captain Remains Ashore: When the "Weisheng" cabins were flooded and the crew and passengers were rescued, they were robbed once by pirates, and the property loss was huge. The captain and chief mate, because they could not stay on the ship, set up tents on the beach and moved ashore. All food was supplied by the "Guangdong" and "Hengsheng" steamships, and they were provided with self-defense weapons, waiting for the salvage ship sent by the company to decide on a plan before coming to Shanghai. Most of the cargo on the ship has been flooded, resulting in huge losses.

Accommodation for the Shipwrecked Personnel: The person who fell into the sea and died was confirmed to be an assistant to the comprador. At that time, the third mate launched a lifeboat to rescue the assistant, but the lifeboat was destroyed by the waves, and the third mate, Xue Mingdeng, drowned. His body has not been found yet. All others are safe. The passengers who were rescued to Shanghai have all returned home. The crew and sailors have also been settled by the company, and the sailors have reported the losses to the union and requested compensation.

Boatman Rescued After an Ordeal

Minli Ferry Shipwrecked in Storm

All Eight Boatmen Fell into the Water

Six Drowned, Two Rescued

Adrift at Sea for Four Days and Nights

The Minli ferry from Fuzhou, with eight crew members, was carrying cargo on the 8th of this month when it encountered a hurricane while sailing in the Beijia waters of Fujian. The storm capsized the boat, and all eight men fell into the water. Six of them were immediately swept away by the huge waves and tragically drowned. Two crew members, Wang Xiansong and Chen Guining, were fortunate enough to grab hold of the guardrail of the boat and held on, avoiding being submerged. However, they were adrift in the vast sea, with no way to call for help. They drifted with the wind and waves for four days and nights. They were exhausted and hoarse, with no strength to hold on. At that critical moment, a British ship (Katie Moller) sailing from Borneo to China came across them and rescued them. The two crew members were injured and mentally exhausted. The ship sailed into the Wusong mouth yesterday morning, and when the foreign affairs section of the municipal public security bureau went to check their passports, the ship's captain handed over the two rescued crew members. The foreign affairs section staff thanked the ship's captain for his kindness in rescuing them, and after completing the inspection, they took the two crew members Wang and Chen back to Wusong and sent them to the Seashore Public Hospital for treatment. Wang Xiansong suffered minor injuries and was discharged from the hospital. The water patrol team sent him to the relief section of the municipal public security bureau to arrange accommodation. Chen Guining was more seriously injured and remained in the hospital for treatment.

Second Refund of Deposits

Since the collapse of Nisshinya Bank, the various deposits and savings in the Grand World Savings Department have been liquidated by accountants Pan Zhaobang and Wu Zheng. Wu Biao Assassination Case

Two Suspects Arrested

The Corpse Was Examined Yesterday

Wu Biao, also known as Wu Baoqing, 34 years old, lived at No. 854 Zuzu Li, Binlang Road. At 8:50 PM the night before last, he was talking with his friends Yu Deyang and Yu Baoquan in his bedroom when a thug with a gun reached out the window and fired, hitting Wu's vital point and killing him. This has already been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The body was transported to the Felun Road Corpse Examination Office. Meanwhile, the Gordon Road Police arrested two suspects, Yu. Yesterday morning, Special Court Inspector Guo Wei visited the office to examine the body. According to Yu Baoquan and Yu Deyang, Yu and Wu were always good friends, and they did not know anything about Wu's shooting. They went to Wu's place that day to discuss something. According to Wu's wife, Wu Wangshi, she was also in the room at the time. After her husband was murdered, he was still able to run to the back hall, and she held him, covered in blood. He only said that he was shot and then fell to the ground and died. Her husband served as deputy captain in the Jiangyin Public Security Bureau from August to December last year and captured two communist bandits. He executed them by firing squad in January of this year. One of the bandits was named Zhu Awu, and he had two brothers, Da Asan and Xiao Asan, who had said that they wanted to murder her husband. After hearing this, Inspector Guo said that the examiner had confirmed that the deceased, Wu Biao, also known as Wu Baoqing, had indeed died from a gunshot wound. The suspects Yu Baoquan and Yu Deyang have been sued by the police station and should be subject to court review. The escaped murderer is being investigated by the police, and the gun is temporarily handed over to the police for safekeeping. The body is handed over to the wife, Wu Wangshi, who will sign and take it back for burial.

Two Trams Collide and Injure People

At around 7 AM yesterday morning, two trams collided on the Bund Baidu Bridge along the Suzhou River. A tram on Route 8 from Yangshupu was coming from Shiliupu. As it was coming off the bridge and turning east, a tram on Route 1 from Jingan Temple Road was winding its way up the Suzhou River and wanted to turn south onto the bridge. However, the driver of Route 8 did not ring the bell, and the driver of Route 1 was in a hurry to drive, and did not pay attention. Suddenly there was a loud noise, and the two cars crashed violently. Sparks flew everywhere. The engine box of the Route 8 tram exploded on the spot, and the front of the car was damaged, and many glass windows were broken. Due to the severe shock, the Route 8 tram derailed. The Route 1 car was also slightly damaged, but was still able to drive. At that time, the passengers in both cars were panicked and scrambled to get off the car, and the order was disrupted. Two male and female passengers were injured and sent to the hospital for treatment. A man had a broken skin on his head, but there was no major problem, while a woman had a chest injury, which was more serious. The derailed Route 8 tram was subsequently ordered by the company to send workers to put it back on the track, but traffic was blocked as a result, and it took more than an hour to restore it.

The Result of Earnest Persuasion by Both Parties' Lawyers

They have also applied to the Special Court to dismiss the case. From now on, this pair of lovebirds will fly their separate ways.

Even Stove Owners are Scared of Extortion

Using a Fruit Basket and "White Golden Dragon" Cigarettes as a Signal

Sure Enough, Someone Contacted [the victim] Near Bubbling Well Road

Lu Ganlang, a native of Haimen, runs a stove shop and rents out rickshaws at 35 Xinji Road. His business is doing well, and he has accumulated some savings, which has attracted the attention of criminals. Between the 3rd and 13th of this month, he suddenly received three threatening letters from a criminal gang, demanding 3,000 yuan. The letters instructed him to book a room at the Wugong Hotel on Fuzhou Road at noon on the 12th, with the surname "Zhou" written on the water sign, and someone would contact him. Lu reported the situation to the Huishan Police Station, which in turn informed the Inspector-General's Office to make an arrest. Detective Sergeant Tang Jian, Detective Liu Shaokui, and Detective Feng Zhiming were dispatched to keep watch, but found nothing. At 9:00 PM, they suddenly received a phone call from the criminals, instructing that the next morning, near the Saposai Road [now Xinzha Road] on Bubbling Well Road in the French Concession, the person should carry a fruit basket and two tins of "White Golden Dragon" cigarettes as a mark. The detectives agreed. The next morning, Detective Feng disguised himself as Lu's representative and followed the instructions. At 11:00 AM, they saw Huang A'mei from Pudong coming forward and asking Feng if he was sent by the Lu family from Zhoujiazui Road. When Feng replied yes, Huang snatched the fruit basket from Feng and was immediately apprehended by Chinese and Western detectives. Upon further interrogation, it was learned that Zhang Zhenya and Zhang Gensong from Pudong were the ones who wrote the threatening letters. The detectives then went to No. 188 Ximen Road and apprehended both Zhangs, taking them back to the Huishan Police Station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special Court. Police lawyer Li Zhishan explained the case, stating that all three defendants had confessed at the police station and requested prosecution. The threatening letters were presented as evidence. Huang A'mei confessed that he was fooled by a friend named Jiang to go there and pick up the fruit and cigarettes, and had not conspired beforehand. The two Zhangs also confessed that Jiang was the one who came up with the idea, saying that Lu was quite wealthy, so they sent a letter asking for a loan of 3,000 yuan. Judge Xiao Xie fen reviewed the confessions and ordered the three defendants to be detained pending sentencing.

Social Affairs Bureau

Order to Western Restaurant Industry to Resume Work Today

Yesterday, the Employer's Absence Led to Failed Mediation

Daily Losses Exceeding 5,000 Yuan

Workers in the city's Western restaurant industry went on strike due to wage and condition issues. The Social Affairs Bureau conducted mediation yesterday, but it failed due to the absence of the employers. It is said that the strike has caused the employers to lose more than 5,000 yuan per day. The union has issued a declaration. The following details are provided regarding tomorrow's situation:

Authorities Mediate: In order to quickly resolve the wage and condition issues in the Western restaurant industry, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau convened a meeting yesterday morning at 10:00 AM to conduct mediation. Union representatives Yao Zhongqing and Wu Shenxiang, Municipal Party Department representative Lu Yin Chu, and Social Affairs Bureau representative Zhang Shuye were present. However, due to the absence of the employer representatives, mediation could not proceed. They had no choice but to ask the labor representatives to return and await legal action. The Western Restaurant Industry Association stated in a letter to the bureau yesterday that they were unable to attend due to time constraints. Last night, the bureau ordered all workers to resume work today and ordered the employer's association to instruct all restaurants not to deliberately make things difficult for the workers when they resume work.

Strike Losses: Western restaurants such as Quanjiafu, Pacific, Royal Palace, Xinlicha, Zuihechun, Yizhixiang, Daguanlou, Hengsheng, Yijia Chun, and Jinlong have been affected by the workers' strike since the afternoon of the 12th. Although they have hired non-union members to work, each restaurant has suffered business losses of more than 5,000 yuan per day. However, the intangible losses of the workers are not included.

District Assistance: Yesterday, the pharmaceutical industry union, the publishing industry union, the medicine industry union, the hotel reception union, the ink making union, the umbrella industry union, the soy sauce industry union, and other unions sent representatives to the Western restaurant industry union to express their condolences, indicating their united support and willingness to act as a backing.

Declaration Issued: All members of the Municipal Western Restaurant Industry Union, being oppressed by the employers and not receiving a sincere response to the proposed terms, have automatically declared a strike. Fathers, elders, brothers, sisters, and comrades from all walks of life, our Western Restaurant Industry Union has been under the oppression of employers for more than ten years. The cost of living is increasing day by day. Our poor workers are not only unable to improve their lives, but their treatment cannot be improved either. These tiger-wolf-like managers are instead exploiting the union's rightful benefits, layer upon layer, and reporting less than the actual amount of our hard-earned small accounts. Wives, concubines, rickshaw drivers, and servants all have to extract from these small accounts. Since 1927, the employer's illegally organized trade association has also extracted its funds from these small accounts, accumulating to as much as seven or eight thousand yuan. These managers also arbitrarily deprive us of the extra money we earn. Continuously dismissing workers and undermining our labor movement is their only trick. This time, in order to demand improved conditions, union representatives have negotiated four times, but there has been no response. They intentionally delay, trying to scatter the hearts of our workers. We ask, how can such vicious methods be tolerated? Therefore, all of our workers, due to the time constraints of the Western restaurant industry, are in a situation of urgency and must promptly demand the establishment of terms. If we are delayed for another year or half a year, our workers will inevitably be dismissed one by one. For this reason, all of our workers, without waiting for the union to mediate, have automatically and painfully risen up since the 12th, and unanimously gone on strike. In this harsh environment, we vow to fight to the end and will not retreat until we have achieved our desired improvements. We ask all sectors to come out and uphold justice for us. This is our declaration.

Yesterday's Summons to the Clerks for a Conversation

Since Wang Huaxing took office as the Director of the Shanghai County Finance Bureau, he has found that the overdue grain tax from the 16th, 17th, 18th, and 19th years of the Republic is very large. Further News on the Election Dispute of the Women's Relief Association

Huang Daping and Four Committee Members Express Resignation

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the election dispute that occurred the other day at the Shanghai Women's Relief Association regarding the election issue, and the names of the elected persons were announced yesterday, the storm seemed to have gradually subsided. However, according to Tang Naixin, Huang Daping, Zhang Xuefei, and Bao Guangyu, four preparatory committee members, the election dispute was superficially about the district representative issue, but the reality was not so. We were ordered to prepare, sacrificing more than two months of time and energy, hoping that all comrades would cooperate sincerely for the welfare of women in the city, but unexpected events occurred. There was one or two individuals who acted independently and disregarded the overall situation. Therefore, although the election has been held, it is better to consider it illegal based on the facts. Women's movement is a cause close to the hearts of women, but this unfortunate situation has occurred. We are truly saddened for the future of the Women's Relief Association and for the women's movement in the city. We have decided to resign from our duties immediately.

Imitating Others' Registered Trademarks

The Government Should Enforce the Law

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce received an instruction from the Social Affairs Bureau stating that the Ministry of Industry ordered an investigation into the act of counterfeiting registered or unregistered trademarks with the intention of deceiving others. (Omission)... Recently, unscrupulous merchants have deliberately misinterpreted the provisions and, taking advantage of the lack of a specific clause for criminal punishment, have dared to counterfeit others' registered trademarks with the intention of profiting. This is a violation of others' rights and should be strictly reprimanded to make them aware that counterfeiting others' registered trademarks should be considered forgery. The order instructs all merchants to comply, and forward this to the trade associations for compliance. etc.
